# // 2025-06-14-19-36-17 (EST)

# Purpose: Comprehensive summons analysis metrics and visualization recommendations for Power BI reporting

## Core Metrics to Track

### 1. **Primary Summons Categories**
- **Parking Summons** (from court data + InfoCop parking counts)
- **Moving Violations** (non-parking summons)
- **Special Complaints** (currently shows 0 - may need different data source)

### 2. **Division/Bureau Breakdown**
Based on your SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT data:
- **Patrol Division** (Platoons A, B, C)
- **Traffic Bureau** (TRF, TCA assignments)
- **Crime Suppression Bureau**
- **Special Operations** (HACSOC)
- **Detectives**
- **School Threat Assessment**

## Key Performance Indicators (KPIs)

### **Volume Metrics**
- Total summons issued (month/YTD)
- Parking vs. Moving violation ratio
- Citations per officer by division
- Top 5 violation types

### **Financial Metrics**
- **Revenue Generated**
  - Fine amounts collected
  - Net revenue (Fine - Court costs)
  - Collection rate % (Paid/Assessed)
- **Revenue by Division**
- **Average fine per violation type**

### **Efficiency Metrics**
- **Summons per officer** (by division)
- **Citations per patrol hour** (if shift data available)
- **Top performers** by division
- **Violation resolution time** (Issue to disposition)

### **Trend Analysis**
- **Month-over-month % change**
- **Day of week patterns**
- **Seasonal trends** (rolling 12-month view)
- **Year-over-year comparisons**

## Power Query Recommendations

### **1. Import Core Tables**
```
SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER (26K rows)
SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT (122 rows)
Title39_Violations (combined lookup)
```

### **2. Create Calculated Measures**
```dax
Total Summons = COUNTROWS(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER)

Parking Summons = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER),
    Title39_Violations[Category] = "Parker"
)

Moving Violations = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER),
    Title39_Violations[Category] IN {"Mover", "Speed"}
)

Net Revenue = 
SUMX(
    SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER,
    [Fine Amount] - [City Cost Amount]
)

Collection Rate = 
DIVIDE(
    SUM(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[Total Paid Amount]),
    SUM(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[Assessed Amount])
)
```

### **3. Date Intelligence**
```dax
// Add to date table
Current Month = [Issue Date] >= STARTOFMONTH(TODAY())
Previous Month = [Issue Date] >= STARTOFMONTH(DATEADD(TODAY(),-1,MONTH))
YTD = [Issue Date] >= STARTOFYEAR(TODAY())
```

## **Daily Breakdown Analysis for May 2025**

**Analyzed data**

````javascript
// Let me create a sample analysis of how day-of-week breakdown would look
// This simulates what you'd see in Power BI

// Sample data structure for May 2025 summons
const mayData = [
    { dayOfWeek: 'Monday', parkingSummons: 45, movingSummons: 12, totalSummons: 57 },
    { dayOfWeek: 'Tuesday', parkingSummons: 52, movingSummons: 18, totalSummons: 70 },
    { dayOfWeek: 'Wednesday', parkingSummons: 48, movingSummons: 15, totalSummons: 63 },
    { dayOfWeek: 'Thursday', parkingSummons: 55, movingSummons: 22, totalSummons: 77 },
    { dayOfWeek: 'Friday', parkingSummons: 62, movingSummons: 28, totalSummons: 90 },
    { dayOfWeek: 'Saturday', parkingSummons: 38, movingSummons: 35, totalSummons: 73 },
    { dayOfWeek: 'Sunday', parkingSummons: 25, movingSummons: 20, totalSummons: 45 }
];

// Calculate totals and percentages
const totals = mayData.reduce((acc, day) => ({
    parking: acc.parking + day.parkingSummons,
    moving: acc.moving + day.movingSummons,
    total: acc.total + day.totalSummons
}), { parking: 0, moving: 0, total: 0 });

console.log("=== MAY 2025 SUMMONS BREAKDOWN BY DAY OF WEEK ===");
console.log("");

mayData.forEach(day => {
    const parkingPct = ((day.parkingSummons / totals.parking) * 100).toFixed(1);
    const movingPct = ((day.movingSummons / totals.moving) * 100).toFixed(1);
    const totalPct = ((day.totalSummons / totals.total) * 100).toFixed(1);
    
    console.log(`${day.dayOfWeek.padEnd(12)} | Parking: ${day.parkingSummons.toString().padStart(3)} (${parkingPct}%) | Moving: ${day.movingSummons.toString().padStart(3)} (${movingPct}%) | Total: ${day.totalSummons.toString().padStart(3)} (${totalPct}%)`);
});

console.log("-".repeat(80));
console.log(`${'TOTALS'.padEnd(12)} | Parking: ${totals.parking.toString().padStart(3)}        | Moving: ${totals.moving.toString().padStart(3)}        | Total: ${totals.total.toString().padStart(3)}`);

console.log("");
console.log("=== KEY INSIGHTS ===");
console.log("â€¢ Highest activity: Friday (enforcement focus)");
console.log("â€¢ Moving violations peak: Saturday (traffic enforcement)");
console.log("â€¢ Parking violations highest: Friday (business district activity)");
console.log("â€¢ Lowest activity: Sunday (reduced enforcement)");
````

## **For Your Power BI Dashboard:**

```
ğŸ“Š Stacked Bar Chart
- X-axis: Day of Week
- Y-axis: Count of Summons
- Legend: Parking vs Moving vs Special Complaints
- Shows patterns like Friday parking peaks, Saturday moving violations
```

### **2. DAX Measures You'll Need:**
```dax
// Day of Week Breakdown
Summons by Day = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER),
    WEEKDAY([Issue Date]) = [Selected Day]
)

// Weekend vs Weekday
Weekend Citations = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER),
    WEEKDAY([Issue Date]) IN {1,7}  // Sunday=1, Saturday=7
)

// Peak Day Analysis
Busiest Day = 
TOPN(1, 
    SUMMARIZE(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER, 
        [Day Name], 
        "Count", COUNTROWS(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER)
    ),
    [Count], DESC
)
```

Perfect! Now I can create the complete InfoCop integration for your Power BI project. This will give you the **real-time summons data** that matches your monthly reports. **InfoCop Power Query Integration for Summons Analysis**

````powerquery
// 2025-06-14-19-36-17 (EST)
// Police_Analytics/InfoCop_Summons_Integration
// Author: R. A. Carucci
// Purpose: Complete InfoCop summons data integration for real-time Power BI reporting

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 1: INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE
// Main summons data with officer, date, and violation type (M, P, C)
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Charge_Date_Case_Type"),
    
    // Filter to .xlsx files only
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    // Transform each Excel file
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                // Clean column types
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Date", type date},
                    {"Summons Type", type text}
                }),
                
                // Clean text fields
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Summons Type", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Summons Type", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Add readable summons categories
                AddedCategory = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Summons Category", each 
                    if [Summons Type] = "M" then "Moving Violation"
                    else if [Summons Type] = "P" then "Parking Violation"
                    else if [Summons Type] = "C" then "Special Complaint"
                    else "Other", type text),
                
                // Add date components for analysis
                AddedMonth = Table.AddColumn(AddedCategory, "Month", each Date.Month([Date]), Int64.Type),
                AddedYear = Table.AddColumn(AddedMonth, "Year", each Date.Year([Date]), Int64.Type),
                AddedMonthName = Table.AddColumn(AddedYear, "Month Name", each Date.MonthName([Date]), type text),
                AddedDayName = Table.AddColumn(AddedMonthName, "Day Name", each Date.DayOfWeekName([Date]), type text),
                AddedWeek = Table.AddColumn(AddedDayName, "Week of Year", each Date.WeekOfYear([Date]), Int64.Type),
                
                // Add month-year for grouping
                AddedMonthYear = Table.AddColumn(AddedWeek, "MONTH_YEAR", each 
                    Date.From(Text.Combine({Text.From([Month]), "/1/", Text.From([Year])})), type date)
            in
                AddedMonthYear
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    // Remove failed files
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    // Expand data from all files
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Date", "Summons Type", "Summons Category", "Month", "Year", 
         "Month Name", "Day Name", "Week of Year", "MONTH_YEAR"}),
    
    // Clean up file metadata columns
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 2: INFOCOP_OFFICER_STREET
// Location data for geographic analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Charge_Date_Street"),
    
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Date", type date},
                    {"Street", type text}
                }),
                
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Standardize street names for analysis
                StandardizedStreets = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Street Cleaned", each 
                    Text.Proper(Text.Replace(Text.Replace([Street], "ST", "Street"), "AVE", "Avenue")), type text)
            in
                StandardizedStreets
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Date", "Street", "Street Cleaned"}),
    
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 3: INFOCOP_OFFICER_STATUTE
// Violation details for citation analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Street_Statute"),
    
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Street", type text},
                    {"Statute", type text}
                }),
                
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Statute", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Statute", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Classify statute types
                AddedStatuteType = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Statute Type", each 
                    if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:4-") then "Moving Violation"
                    else if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:8-") then "Parking Violation"
                    else if Text.Contains([Statute], "Speed") then "Speed Violation"
                    else if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:3-") then "Equipment/Registration"
                    else if Text.Length([Statute]) > 0 then "City Ordinance"
                    else "Other", type text)
            in
                AddedStatuteType
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Street", "Statute", "Statute Type"}),
    
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 4: INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS
// Combined data for comprehensive analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    ChargeData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content],
    StreetData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_STREET"]}[Content],
    StatuteData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_STATUTE"]}[Content],
    AssignmentData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT"]}[Content],
    
    // Join charge data with street data
    JoinedWithStreets = Table.NestedJoin(ChargeData, {"Officer Name", "Date"}, 
                                       StreetData, {"Officer Name", "Date"}, 
                                       "StreetInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    ExpandedStreets = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithStreets, "StreetInfo", {"Street", "Street Cleaned"}),
    
    // Join with statute data
    JoinedWithStatutes = Table.NestedJoin(ExpandedStreets, {"Officer Name", "Street"}, 
                                        StatuteData, {"Officer Name", "Street"}, 
                                        "StatuteInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    ExpandedStatutes = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithStatutes, "StatuteInfo", {"Statute", "Statute Type"}),
    
    // Convert officer names to badge numbers for assignment lookup
    // This assumes officer names can be matched to assignments - may need adjustment
    AddedBadgeNumber = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedStatutes, "Badge Number", each 
        // This will need to be customized based on your name-to-badge mapping
        "TBD", type text),
    
    // Join with assignment data
    JoinedWithAssignments = Table.NestedJoin(AddedBadgeNumber, {"Badge Number"}, 
                                           AssignmentData, {"BADGE#"}, 
                                           "AssignmentInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    ExpandedAssignments = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithAssignments, "AssignmentInfo", 
        {"PATROL_MEMBER", "ASSIGNMENT", "RANK", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit Group"}),
    
    // Add validation flags
    AddedValidation = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedAssignments, "Data Quality", each 
        if [Street] = null then "Missing Location"
        else if [Statute] = null then "Missing Statute"
        else if [PATROL_MEMBER] = null then "Unassigned Officer"
        else "Complete", type text)
in
    AddedValidation

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 5: MONTHLY_SUMMONS_SUMMARY
// Executive dashboard summary matching your monthly report format
// ===================================================================

let
    InfoCopData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS"]}[Content],
    CurrentMonth = Date.Month(Date.From(DateTime.LocalNow())),
    CurrentYear = Date.Year(Date.From(DateTime.LocalNow())),
    
    // Filter to current month
    CurrentMonthData = Table.SelectRows(InfoCopData, each [Year] = CurrentYear and [Month] = CurrentMonth),
    
    // Summary by summons type
    SummaryByType = Table.Group(CurrentMonthData, {"Summons Type"}, {
        {"Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // Summary by division
    SummaryByDivision = Table.Group(CurrentMonthData, {"Platoon"}, {
        {"Parking_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "P")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Moving_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "M")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Special_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "C")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Total_Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // Create final summary matching report format
    FinalSummary = Table.FromRows({
        {"Parking Summons", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "P")[Count] ? ? {0})},
        {"Non-Parking Summons", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "M")[Count] ? ? {0})},
        {"Special Complaints", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "C")[Count] ? ? {0})}
    }, {"Summons Type", "Count"})
in
    FinalSummary
````

## Response:
6/14/2025, 5:06:48 PM

Perfect! Now I can see your data structure. The InfoCop exports have **officer names only** (no badge numbers), so I need to modify the integration approach. **InfoCop Power Query Integration for Summons Analysis** âˆ™ Version 2

````powerquery
// 2025-06-14-19-36-17 (EST)
// Police_Analytics/InfoCop_Summons_Integration
// Author: R. A. Carucci
// Purpose: Complete InfoCop summons data integration for real-time Power BI reporting

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 1: INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE
// Main summons data with officer, date, and violation type (M, P, C)
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Charge_Date_Case_Type"),
    
    // Filter to .xlsx files only
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    // Transform each Excel file
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                // Clean column types
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Date", type date},
                    {"Summons Type", type text}
                }),
                
                // Clean text fields
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Summons Type", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Summons Type", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Add readable summons categories
                AddedCategory = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Summons Category", each 
                    if [Summons Type] = "M" then "Moving Violation"
                    else if [Summons Type] = "P" then "Parking Violation"
                    else if [Summons Type] = "C" then "Special Complaint"
                    else "Other", type text),
                
                // Add date components for analysis
                AddedMonth = Table.AddColumn(AddedCategory, "Month", each Date.Month([Date]), Int64.Type),
                AddedYear = Table.AddColumn(AddedMonth, "Year", each Date.Year([Date]), Int64.Type),
                AddedMonthName = Table.AddColumn(AddedYear, "Month Name", each Date.MonthName([Date]), type text),
                AddedDayName = Table.AddColumn(AddedMonthName, "Day Name", each Date.DayOfWeekName([Date]), type text),
                AddedWeek = Table.AddColumn(AddedDayName, "Week of Year", each Date.WeekOfYear([Date]), Int64.Type),
                
                // Add month-year for grouping
                AddedMonthYear = Table.AddColumn(AddedWeek, "MONTH_YEAR", each 
                    Date.From(Text.Combine({Text.From([Month]), "/1/", Text.From([Year])})), type date)
            in
                AddedMonthYear
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    // Remove failed files
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    // Expand data from all files
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Date", "Summons Type", "Summons Category", "Month", "Year", 
         "Month Name", "Day Name", "Week of Year", "MONTH_YEAR"}),
    
    // Clean up file metadata columns
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 2: INFOCOP_OFFICER_STREET
// Location data for geographic analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Charge_Date_Street"),
    
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Date", type date},
                    {"Street", type text}
                }),
                
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Standardize street names for analysis
                StandardizedStreets = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Street Cleaned", each 
                    Text.Proper(Text.Replace(Text.Replace([Street], "ST", "Street"), "AVE", "Avenue")), type text)
            in
                StandardizedStreets
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Date", "Street", "Street Cleaned"}),
    
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 3: INFOCOP_OFFICER_STATUTE
// Violation details for citation analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Street_Statute"),
    
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Street", type text},
                    {"Statute", type text}
                }),
                
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Statute", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Statute", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Classify statute types
                AddedStatuteType = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Statute Type", each 
                    if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:4-") then "Moving Violation"
                    else if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:8-") then "Parking Violation"
                    else if Text.Contains([Statute], "Speed") then "Speed Violation"
                    else if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:3-") then "Equipment/Registration"
                    else if Text.Length([Statute]) > 0 then "City Ordinance"
                    else "Other", type text)
            in
                AddedStatuteType
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Street", "Statute", "Statute Type"}),
    
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 4: INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS
// Combined data for comprehensive analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    ChargeData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content],
    StreetData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_STREET"]}[Content],
    StatuteData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_STATUTE"]}[Content],
    AssignmentData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT"]}[Content],
    
    // Join charge data with street data
    JoinedWithStreets = Table.NestedJoin(ChargeData, {"Officer Name", "Date"}, 
                                       StreetData, {"Officer Name", "Date"}, 
                                       "StreetInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    ExpandedStreets = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithStreets, "StreetInfo", {"Street", "Street Cleaned"}),
    
    // Join with statute data
    JoinedWithStatutes = Table.NestedJoin(ExpandedStreets, {"Officer Name", "Street"}, 
                                        StatuteData, {"Officer Name", "Street"}, 
                                        "StatuteInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    ExpandedStatutes = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithStatutes, "StatuteInfo", {"Statute", "Statute Type"}),
    
    // Join with assignment data using officer names
    // InfoCop uses officer names, assignment data has PATROL_MEMBER names
    JoinedWithAssignments = Table.NestedJoin(ExpandedStatutes, {"Officer Name"}, 
                                           AssignmentData, {"PATROL_MEMBER"}, 
                                           "AssignmentInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    ExpandedAssignments = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithAssignments, "AssignmentInfo", 
        {"PATROL_MEMBER", "ASSIGNMENT", "RANK", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit Group"}),
    
    // Add validation flags
    AddedValidation = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedAssignments, "Data Quality", each 
        if [Street] = null then "Missing Location"
        else if [Statute] = null then "Missing Statute"
        else if [PATROL_MEMBER] = null then "Unassigned Officer"
        else "Complete", type text)
in
    AddedValidation

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 5: MONTHLY_SUMMONS_SUMMARY
// Executive dashboard summary matching your monthly report format
// ===================================================================

let
    InfoCopData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS"]}[Content],
    CurrentMonth = Date.Month(Date.From(DateTime.LocalNow())),
    CurrentYear = Date.Year(Date.From(DateTime.LocalNow())),
    
    // Filter to current month
    CurrentMonthData = Table.SelectRows(InfoCopData, each [Year] = CurrentYear and [Month] = CurrentMonth),
    
    // Summary by summons type
    SummaryByType = Table.Group(CurrentMonthData, {"Summons Type"}, {
        {"Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // Summary by division
    SummaryByDivision = Table.Group(CurrentMonthData, {"Platoon"}, {
        {"Parking_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "P")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Moving_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "M")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Special_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "C")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Total_Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // Create final summary matching report format
    FinalSummary = Table.FromRows({
        {"Parking Summons", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "P")[Count] ? ? {0})},
        {"Non-Parking Summons", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "M")[Count] ? ? {0})},
        {"Special Complaints", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "C")[Count] ? ? {0})}
    }, {"Summons Type", "Count"})
in
    FinalSummary
````

## **Key Integration Strategy Update:**

Since InfoCop exports use **officer names** instead of badge numbers, I've updated the query to join on:
- **InfoCop Data:** `Officer Name` 
- **Assignment Data:** `PATROL_MEMBER`

## **Power BI Implementation Steps:**

### **1. Import These 5 Key Queries:**
```
1. INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE (M, P, C counts)
2. SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT (Division assignments) 
3. SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER (Revenue data)
4. Title39_Data (Violation lookup)
5. INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS (Combined analysis)
```

### **2. Create DAX Measures for May 2025 Analysis:**
```dax
// Day of Week Breakdown
May_Parking_Monday = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "P",
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] = "Monday"
)

// Division Performance
Citations_by_Platoon = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS),
    INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS[Platoon] <> BLANK()
)

// Monthly Summary (matching your report format)
Total_Parking_Summons = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "P"
)
```

### **4. Name Matching Considerations:**

**Potential Issues:**
- Officer name formats may differ between InfoCop and assignment data
- Middle initials, nicknames, or spelling variations
- Retired/transferred officers in one system but not the other

**Solution:**
Add a **name standardization step** in the Power Query:
```powerquery
// Standardize officer names for better matching
StandardizedName = Table.AddColumn(CleanedFields, "Officer Name Std", each 
    Text.Proper(Text.Trim(Text.Replace([Officer Name], "  ", " "))), type text)
```

## ğŸ”§ DAX MEASURES FOR MAY 2025 ANALYSIS

```dax
// ============================================
// DAY OF WEEK MEASURES
// ============================================

May_2025_Total = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025
)

May_Parking_Monday = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "P",
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] = "Monday
````



## Prompt:
6/14/2025, 5:09:53 PM

Continue



## Response:
6/14/2025, 5:11:49 PM



**undefined**

````plaintext
May_Parking_Monday = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "P",
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] = "Monday"
)

May_Moving_Saturday = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "M",
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] = "Saturday"
)

// ============================================
// DIVISION PERFORMANCE MEASURES
// ============================================

Citations_by_Platoon = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS),
    INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS[Platoon] <> BLANK()
)

Traffic_Division_Total = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS),
    INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS[Platoon] = "Traffic"
)

Citations_Per_Officer = 
DIVIDE(
    [Citations_by_Platoon],
    CALCULATE(
        DISTINCTCOUNT(INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS[Officer Name]),
        INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS[Platoon] <> BLANK()
    ),
    0
)

// ============================================
// REVENUE MEASURES (Integration with Court Data)
// ============================================

Total_Revenue_Generated = 
SUMX(
    SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER,
    SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[Fine Amount] - SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[City Cost Amount]
)

Collection_Rate = 
DIVIDE(
    SUM(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[Total Paid Amount]),
    SUM(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[Assessed Amount]),
    0
) * 100

Average_Fine_Amount = 
AVERAGE(SUMMONS_COURT_MASTER[Fine Amount])

// ============================================
// TREND ANALYSIS MEASURES
// ============================================

Previous_Month_Citations = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    DATEADD(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Date], -1, MONTH)
)

Month_over_Month_Change = 
DIVIDE(
    [May_2025_Total] - [Previous_Month_Citations],
    [Previous_Month_Citations],
    0
) * 100

YTD_Citations = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    DATESYTD(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Date])
)

// ============================================
// VIOLATION TYPE BREAKDOWN
// ============================================

Parking_Percentage = 
DIVIDE(
    CALCULATE(
        COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
        INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "P"
    ),
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    0
) * 100

Moving_Percentage = 
DIVIDE(
    CALCULATE(
        COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
        INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "M"
    ),
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    0
) * 100

Special_Complaints_Count = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "C"
)

// ============================================
// TOP PERFORMERS MEASURES
// ============================================

Officer_Citation_Count = 
COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE)

Officer_Rank = 
RANKX(
    ALL(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Officer Name]),
    [Officer_Citation_Count],
    ,
    DESC
)

Top_10_Officers = 
IF([Officer_Rank] <= 10, [Officer_Citation_Count], BLANK())

// ============================================
// EFFICIENCY METRICS
// ============================================

Division_Efficiency_Rating = 
SWITCH(
    TRUE(),
    [Citations_Per_Officer] >= 20, "High",
    [Citations_Per_Officer] >= 10, "Medium",
    "Low"
)

Weekend_vs_Weekday = 
VAR WeekendCitations = 
    CALCULATE(
        COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
        INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] IN {"Saturday", "Sunday"}
    )
VAR Weekdaycitations = 
    CALCULATE(
        COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
        NOT(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] IN {"Saturday", "Sunday"})
    )
RETURN
    DIVIDE(WeekendCitations, Weekdaycitations, 0)
```

## ğŸ› ï¸ NAME STANDARDIZATION QUERY

```powerquery
// ============================================
// OFFICER NAME STANDARDIZATION
// ============================================

let
    Source = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content],
    
    // Standardize officer names for better matching
    StandardizedNames = Table.AddColumn(Source, "Officer Name Standardized", each
        let
            CleanName = Text.Trim(Text.Clean([Officer Name])),
            ProperCase = Text.Proper(CleanName),
            // Handle common name variations
            RemoveMiddleInitials = Text.Replace(Text.Replace(ProperCase, " Jr.", ""), " Sr.", ""),
            RemoveExtraSpaces = Text.Replace(RemoveExtraSpaces, "  ", " ")
        in
            RemoveExtraSpaces
    , type text),
    
    // Create lookup table for manual name corrections
    NameMappingTable = Table.FromRows({
        {"Johnson, Michael", "Johnson, Mike"},
        {"Williams, Robert", "Williams, Rob"},
        {"Smith, Jonathan", "Smith, John"}
        // Add more mappings as needed
    }, {"InfoCop_Name", "Assignment_Name"}),
    
    // Apply manual corrections
    ApplyMappings = Table.AddColumn(StandardizedNames, "Final_Officer_Name", each
        let
            LookupResult = Table.SelectRows(NameMappingTable, each [InfoCop_Name] = [Officer Name Standardized])
        in
            if Table.RowCount(LookupResult) > 0 
            then LookupResult{0}[Assignment_Name]
            else [Officer Name Standardized]
    , type text)
in
    ApplyMappings
```

### **Color Palette:**
- **Primary Blue:** #1f4e79 (HPD branding)
- **Secondary Gold:** #ffc000 (HPD accent)
- **Success Green:** #70ad47
- **Warning Orange:** #ff8c00
- **Danger Red:** #c5504b
- **Neutral Gray:** #7f7f7f

### **Typography:**
- **Headers:** Segoe UI Bold, 16-24pt
- **Body Text:** Segoe UI Regular, 10-12pt
- **KPI Numbers:** Segoe UI Bold, 18-28pt

### **Interactive Elements:**
- **Drill-through:** Click division â†’ officer detail
- **Cross-filtering:** Select day â†’ filter all visuals
- **Tooltips:** Hover for additional context
- **Bookmarks:** Save specific views/filters

### **Refresh Schedule:**
- **Real-time:** KPI cards (5-minute refresh)
- **Daily:** Trend charts (midnight refresh)
- **Weekly:** Historical comparisons
- **Monthly:** Full data validation

This comprehensive layout gives you **executive oversight**, **operational management**, **performance tracking**, **financial analysis**, and **mobile accessibility** - everything needed for modern police analytics! ````

// ============================================
// DAY OF WEEK MEASURES
// ============================================

May_2025_Total = 
CALCULATE(
    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025
)

May_Parking_Monday =

    COUNTROWS(INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE),
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Summons Type] = "P",
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Month] = 5,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Year] = 2025,
    INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE[Day Name] = "Monday
````

Perfect! Now let me create the name standardization query as a separate artifact:

**Officer Name Standardization Query**

````powerquery
// 2025-06-14-19-36-17 (EST)
// Police_Analytics/Officer_Name_Standardization
// Author: R. A. Carucci
// Purpose: Standardize officer names between InfoCop and assignment data for accurate matching

// ===================================================================
// QUERY: OFFICER_NAME_STANDARDIZATION
// Handles name variations, nicknames, and format differences
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content],
    
    // Step 1: Basic text cleaning
    CleanedNames = Table.AddColumn(Source, "Officer Name Cleaned", each
        Text.Trim(Text.Clean(Text.Replace([Officer Name], "  ", " "))), type text),
    
    // Step 2: Convert to proper case
    ProperCase = Table.AddColumn(CleanedNames, "Officer Name Proper", each
        Text.Proper([Officer Name Cleaned]), type text),
    
    // Step 3: Handle common suffixes and titles
    RemoveSuffixes = Table.AddColumn(ProperCase, "Name Without Suffixes", each
        let
            Step1 = Text.Replace([Officer Name Proper], " Jr.", ""),
            Step2 = Text.Replace(Step1, " Sr.", ""),
            Step3 = Text.Replace(Step2, " III", ""),
            Step4 = Text.Replace(Step3, " II", ""),
            Step5 = Text.Replace(Step4, "Officer ", ""),
            Step6 = Text.Replace(Step5, "Ofc. ", ""),
            Step7 = Text.Replace(Step6, "P.O. ", "")
        in
            Text.Trim(Step7), type text),
    
    // Step 4: Create nickname mapping table
    NicknameMappings = Table.FromRows({
        // Common police department name variations
        {"Michael", "Mike"},
        {"Robert", "Rob"},
        {"Robert", "Bob"},
        {"Richard", "Rich"},
        {"Richard", "Rick"},
        {"William", "Bill"},
        {"William", "Will"},
        {"James", "Jim"},
        {"James", "Jimmy"},
        {"Christopher", "Chris"},
        {"Anthony", "Tony"},
        {"Joseph", "Joe"},
        {"Thomas", "Tom"},
        {"Daniel", "Dan"},
        {"Matthew", "Matt"},
        {"John", "Johnny"},
        {"David", "Dave"},
        {"Jennifer", "Jen"},
        {"Elizabeth", "Liz"},
        {"Elizabeth", "Beth"},
        {"Catherine", "Cathy"},
        {"Margaret", "Maggie"},
        {"Margaret", "Peggy"},
        {"Patricia", "Pat"},
        {"Christine", "Chris"},
        {"Stephanie", "Steph"}
    }, {"Full_Name", "Nickname"}),
    
    // Step 5: Handle Last Name, First Name format
    StandardizeFormat = Table.AddColumn(RemoveSuffixes, "Standardized_Name", each
        let
            NameParts = Text.Split([Name Without Suffixes], ","),
            HasComma = List.Count(NameParts) > 1
        in
            if HasComma then
                // Already in "Last, First" format - just clean it up
                Text.Trim(NameParts{0}) & ", " & Text.Trim(NameParts{1})
            else
                // Try to split "First Last" and convert to "Last, First"
                let
                    SpaceParts = Text.Split([Name Without Suffixes], " "),
                    PartCount = List.Count(SpaceParts)
                in
                    if PartCount >= 2 then
                        // Assume last part is last name, everything else is first/middle
                        let
                            LastName = SpaceParts{PartCount - 1},
                            FirstNames = Text.Combine(List.FirstN(SpaceParts, PartCount - 1), " ")
                        in
                            LastName & ", " & FirstNames
                    else
                        [Name Without Suffixes]
        , type text),
    
    // Step 6: Apply nickname substitutions
    ApplyNicknames = Table.AddColumn(StandardizeFormat, "Final_Officer_Name", each
        let
            CurrentName = [Standardized_Name],
            // Check if we need to replace any nicknames with full names
            NameParts = Text.Split(CurrentName, ", "),
            LastName = if List.Count(NameParts) > 0 then NameParts{0} else "",
            FirstPart = if List.Count(NameParts) > 1 then NameParts{1} else "",
            FirstNames = Text.Split(FirstPart, " "),
            FirstName = if List.Count(FirstNames) > 0 then FirstNames{0} else "",
            
            // Look up potential full name for nickname
            NicknameCheck = Table.SelectRows(NicknameMappings, each [Nickname] = FirstName),
            
            FinalName = if Table.RowCount(NicknameCheck) > 0 then
                // Found a nickname match - create both versions for lookup
                let
                    FullNameVersion = LastName & ", " & NicknameCheck{0}[Full_Name],
                    // Keep the original for now - we'll handle matching logic later
                    ResultName = CurrentName
                in
                    ResultName
            else
                CurrentName
        in
            FinalName, type text),
    
    // Step 7: Create fuzzy matching score for assignment data
    CreateMatchingTable = Table.AddColumn(ApplyNicknames, "Matching_Variations", each
        let
            BaseName = [Final_Officer_Name],
            NameParts = Text.Split(BaseName, ", "),
            LastName = if List.Count(NameParts) > 0 then NameParts{0} else "",
            FirstPart = if List.Count(NameParts) > 1 then NameParts{1} else "",
            FirstNames = Text.Split(FirstPart, " "),
            FirstName = if List.Count(FirstNames) > 0 then FirstNames{0} else "",
            MiddleName = if List.Count(FirstNames) > 1 then FirstNames{1} else "",
            
            // Create possible variations for matching
            Variations = {
                BaseName,  // Original
                LastName & ", " & FirstName,  // Just first and last
                FirstName & " " & LastName,   // First Last format
                LastName & "," & FirstName,   // No space after comma
                Text.Upper(BaseName),         // All caps
                Text.Lower(BaseName)          // All lowercase
            }
        in
            Text.Combine(Variations, "|"), type text),
    
    // Step 8: Remove intermediate columns and finalize
    FinalResult = Table.SelectColumns(CreateMatchingTable, {
        "Officer Name",           // Original
        "Date", 
        "Summons Type", 
        "Summons Category",
        "Final_Officer_Name",     // Standardized
        "Matching_Variations"     // For fuzzy matching
    })
in
    FinalResult

// ===================================================================
// SUPPLEMENTARY QUERY: ASSIGNMENT_NAME_LOOKUP
// Creates a matching table for assignment data
// ===================================================================

let
    AssignmentSource = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT"]}[Content],
    
    // Apply same standardization to assignment names
    StandardizedAssignments = Table.AddColumn(AssignmentSource, "Assignment_Name_Std", each
        let
            CleanName = Text.Trim(Text.Clean([PATROL_MEMBER])),
            ProperCase = Text.Proper(Cl
````

// SUPPLEMENTARY QUERY: ASSIGNMENT_NAME_LOOKUP
// Creates a matching table for assignment data
// ===================================================================

let
    AssignmentSource = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT"]}[Content],
    
    // Apply same standardization to assignment names
    StandardizedAssignments = Table.AddColumn(AssignmentSource, "Assignment_Name_Std", each
        let
            CleanName = Text.Trim(Text.Clean([PATROL_MEMBER])),
            ProperCase = Text.Proper(CleanName),
            RemoveTitles = Text.Replace(Text.Replace(ProperCase, "Officer ", ""), "P.O.

", ""),
            
            // Convert to Last, First format if needed
            NameParts = Text.Split(RemoveTitles, ","),
            HasComma = List.Count(NameParts) > 1
        in
            if HasComma then
                Text.Trim(NameParts{0}) & ", " & Text.Trim(NameParts{1})
            else
                let
                    SpaceParts = Text.Split(RemoveTitles, " "),
                    PartCount = List.Count(SpaceParts)
                in
                    if PartCount >= 2 then
                        let
                            LastName = SpaceParts{PartCount - 1},
                            FirstNames = Text.Combine(List.FirstN(SpaceParts, PartCount - 1), " ")
                        in
                            LastName & ", " & FirstNames
                    else
                        RemoveTitles
        , type text)
in
    StandardizedAssignments

// ===================================================================
// MASTER QUERY: ENHANCED_INFOCOP_INTEGRATION
// Updated integration with improved name matching
// ===================================================================

let
    InfoCopData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="OFFICER_NAME_STANDARDIZATION"]}[Content],
    AssignmentData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="ASSIGNMENT_NAME_LOOKUP"]}[Content],
    
    // First attempt: Direct name match
    DirectMatch = Table.NestedJoin(InfoCopData, {"Final_Officer_Name"}, 
                                 AssignmentData, {"Assignment_Name_Std"}, 
                                 "DirectMatchInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    
    // Add fuzzy matching for unmatched records
    FuzzyMatchLogic = Table.AddColumn(DirectMatch, "Best_Match", each
        let
            DirectResult = [DirectMatchInfo],
            HasDirectMatch = Table.RowCount(DirectResult) > 0 and DirectResult{0}[PATROL_MEMBER]? <> null
        in
            if HasDirectMatch then
                DirectResult{0}
            else
                // Implement fuzzy matching logic
                let
                    InfoCopName = [Final_Officer_Name],
                    InfoCopParts = Text.Split(InfoCopName, ", "),
                    InfoCopLast = if List.Count(InfoCopParts) > 0 then InfoCopParts{0} else "",
                    InfoCopFirst = if List.Count(InfoCopParts) > 1 then Text.Split(InfoCopParts{1}, " "){0} else "",
                    
                    // Find best matches by last name similarity
                    LastNameMatches = Table.SelectRows(AssignmentData, each 
                        Text.Contains(Text.Upper([Assignment_Name_Std]), Text.Upper(InfoCopLast))
                    ),
                    
                    // If we found last name matches, check first name
                    BestMatch = if Table.RowCount(LastNameMatches) > 0 then
                        let
                            FirstNameMatches = Table.SelectRows(LastNameMatches, each
                                Text.Contains(Text.Upper([Assignment_Name_Std]), Text.Upper(InfoCopFirst))
                            )
                        in
                            if Table.RowCount(FirstNameMatches) > 0 then
                                FirstNameMatches{0}
                            else
                                LastNameMatches{0}  // Take first last name match
                    else
                        null
                in
                    BestMatch
        , type record),
    
    // Expand the best match results
    ExpandedMatches = Table.ExpandRecordColumn(FuzzyMatchLogic, "Best_Match", 
        {"PATROL_MEMBER", "ASSIGNMENT", "RANK", "BADGE#", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit Group"}),
    
    // Add match quality indicators
    MatchQuality = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedMatches, "Match_Quality", each
        let
            HasDirectMatch = Table.RowCount([DirectMatchInfo]) > 0 and [DirectMatchInfo]{0}[PATROL_MEMBER]? <> null,
            HasAssignment = [PATROL_MEMBER] <> null
        in
            if HasDirectMatch then "EXACT"
            else if HasAssignment then "FUZZY"
            else "NO_MATCH"
        , type text),
    
    // Add data quality flags
    DataQualityFlags = Table.AddColumn(MatchQuality, "Data_Quality_Issues", each
        let
            Issues = {}
        in
            if [Match_Quality] = "NO_MATCH" then Issues & {"Unmatched Officer"}
            else if [Match_Quality] = "FUZZY" then Issues & {"Fuzzy Match - Verify"}
            else if [ASSIGNMENT] = null then Issues & {"Missing Assignment"}
            else {}
        , type list),
    
    // Clean up columns
    FinalResult = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedMatches, {"DirectMatchInfo", "Matching_Variations"})
in
    FinalResult

// ===================================================================
// VALIDATION QUERY: NAME_MATCHING_REPORT
// Quality control report for name matching results
// ===================================================================

let
    EnhancedData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="ENHANCED_INFOCOP_INTEGRATION"]}[Content],
    
    // Summary by match quality
    MatchQualitySummary = Table.Group(EnhancedData, {"Match_Quality"}, {
        {"Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type},
        {"Percentage", each (Table.RowCount(_) / Table.RowCount(EnhancedData)) * 100, type number}
    }),
    
    // List of unmatched officers
    UnmatchedOfficers = Table.SelectRows(EnhancedData, each [Match_Quality] = "NO_MATCH"),
    UnmatchedSummary = Table.Group(UnmatchedOfficers, {"Final_Officer_Name"}, {
        {"Citation_Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // List of fuzzy matches for review
    FuzzyMatches = Table.SelectRows(EnhancedData, each [Match_Quality] = "FUZZY"),
    FuzzyReview = Table.SelectColumns(FuzzyMatches, {
        "Officer Name", "Final_Officer_Name", "PATROL_MEMBER", "ASSIGNMENT", "Citation_Count"
    }),
    
    // Create validation report
    ValidationReport = Table.FromRows({
        {"Total Records", Table.RowCount(EnhancedData)},
        {"Exact Matches", Table.RowCount(Table.SelectRows(EnhancedData, each [Match_Quality] = "EXACT"))},
        {"Fuzzy Matches", Table.RowCount(Table.SelectRows(EnhancedData, each [Match_Quality] = "FUZZY"))},
        {"No Matches", Table.RowCount(Table.SelectRows(EnhancedData, each [Match_Quality] = "NO_MATCH"))},
        {"Match Success Rate", (Table.RowCount(Table.SelectRows(EnhancedData, each [Match_Quality] <> "NO_MATCH")) / Table.RowCount(EnhancedData)) * 100}
    }, {"Metric", "Value"})
in
    ValidationReport

// ===================================================================
// MANUAL OVERRIDE TABLE (Optional)
// For handling special cases and corrections
// ===================================================================

let
    // Create a manual mapping table for problem cases
    ManualMappings = Table.FromRows({
        // InfoCop Name, Assignment Name, Notes
        {"Smith, Jon", "Smith, John", "Missing 'h' in InfoCop"},
        {"Johnson, Mike", "Johnson, Michael", "Nickname vs Full Name"},
        {"Williams, Bob", "Williams, Robert", "Nickname vs Full Name"},
        {"Brown, Chris", "Brown, Christopher", "Nickname vs Full Name"},
        {"Davis, Rich", "Davis, Richard", "Nickname vs Full Name"}
        // Add more manual corrections as needed
    }, {"InfoCop_Name", "Assignment_Name", "Notes"}),
    
    // Apply data types
    TypedMappings = Table.TransformColumnTypes(ManualMappings, {
        {"InfoCop_Name", type text},
        {"Assignment_Name", type text},
        {"Notes", type text}
    })
in
    TypedMappings
````

**InfoCop Power Query Integration for Summons Analysis** âˆ™ Version 3

````powerquery
// 2025-06-14-19-36-17 (EST)
// Police_Analytics/InfoCop_Summons_Integration
// Author: R. A. Carucci
// Purpose: Complete InfoCop summons data integration for real-time Power BI reporting

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 1: INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE
// Main summons data with officer, date, and violation type (M, P, C)
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Charge_Date_Case_Type"),
    
    // Filter to .xlsx files only
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    // Transform each Excel file
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                // Clean column types
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Date", type date},
                    {"Summons Type", type text}
                }),
                
                // Clean text fields
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Summons Type", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Summons Type", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Add readable summons categories
                AddedCategory = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Summons Category", each 
                    if [Summons Type] = "M" then "Moving Violation"
                    else if [Summons Type] = "P" then "Parking Violation"
                    else if [Summons Type] = "C" then "Special Complaint"
                    else "Other", type text),
                
                // Add date components for analysis
                AddedMonth = Table.AddColumn(AddedCategory, "Month", each Date.Month([Date]), Int64.Type),
                AddedYear = Table.AddColumn(AddedMonth, "Year", each Date.Year([Date]), Int64.Type),
                AddedMonthName = Table.AddColumn(AddedYear, "Month Name", each Date.MonthName([Date]), type text),
                AddedDayName = Table.AddColumn(AddedMonthName, "Day Name", each Date.DayOfWeekName([Date]), type text),
                AddedWeek = Table.AddColumn(AddedDayName, "Week of Year", each Date.WeekOfYear([Date]), Int64.Type),
                
                // Add month-year for grouping
                AddedMonthYear = Table.AddColumn(AddedWeek, "MONTH_YEAR", each 
                    Date.From(Text.Combine({Text.From([Month]), "/1/", Text.From([Year])})), type date)
            in
                AddedMonthYear
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    // Remove failed files
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    // Expand data from all files
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Date", "Summons Type", "Summons Category", "Month", "Year", 
         "Month Name", "Day Name", "Week of Year", "MONTH_YEAR"}),
    
    // Clean up file metadata columns
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 2: INFOCOP_OFFICER_STREET
// Location data for geographic analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Charge_Date_Street"),
    
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Date", type date},
                    {"Street", type text}
                }),
                
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Standardize street names for analysis
                StandardizedStreets = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Street Cleaned", each 
                    Text.Proper(Text.Replace(Text.Replace([Street], "ST", "Street"), "AVE", "Avenue")), type text)
            in
                StandardizedStreets
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Date", "Street", "Street Cleaned"}),
    
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 3: INFOCOP_OFFICER_STATUTE
// Violation details for citation analysis
// ===================================================================

let
    Source = Folder.Files("C:\Users\carucci_r\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\_MONTHLY_DATA\_EXPORTS\Summons\INFOCOP\Officer_Street_Statute"),
    
    FilteredFiles = Table.SelectRows(Source, each 
        [Attributes]?[Hidden]? <> true and 
        Text.EndsWith([Name], ".xlsx")
    ),
    
    TransformFiles = Table.AddColumn(FilteredFiles, "Data", each
        try 
            let
                ExcelFile = Excel.Workbook([Content], null, true),
                FirstSheet = ExcelFile{0}[Data],
                PromotedHeaders = Table.PromoteHeaders(FirstSheet, [PromoteAllScalars=true]),
                
                CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PromotedHeaders,{
                    {"Officer Name", type text},
                    {"Street", type text},
                    {"Statute", type text}
                }),
                
                CleanedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Clean, type text},
                    {"Statute", Text.Clean, type text}
                }),
                
                TrimmedFields = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedFields,{
                    {"Officer Name", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Street", Text.Trim, type text},
                    {"Statute", Text.Trim, type text}
                }),
                
                // Classify statute types
                AddedStatuteType = Table.AddColumn(TrimmedFields, "Statute Type", each 
                    if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:4-") then "Moving Violation"
                    else if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:8-") then "Parking Violation"
                    else if Text.Contains([Statute], "Speed") then "Speed Violation"
                    else if Text.StartsWith([Statute], "39:3-") then "Equipment/Registration"
                    else if Text.Length([Statute]) > 0 then "City Ordinance"
                    else "Other", type text)
            in
                AddedStatuteType
        otherwise null
    ),
    
    FilteredTransforms = Table.SelectRows(TransformFiles, each [Data] <> null),
    
    ExpandedData = Table.ExpandTableColumn(FilteredTransforms, "Data", 
        {"Officer Name", "Street", "Statute", "Statute Type"}),
    
    CleanedColumns = Table.RemoveColumns(ExpandedData, 
        {"Name", "Extension", "Date accessed", "Date modified", "Date created", "Attributes", "Folder Path", "Content"}, 
        MissingField.Ignore)
in
    CleanedColumns

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 4: INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS (SIMPLIFIED VERSION)
// Combined data for comprehensive analysis - Fixed for single table approach
// ===================================================================

let
    // Start with main charge data
    ChargeData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content],
    AssignmentData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT"]}[Content],
    
    // Simple join with assignment data using officer names
    // Use exact name matching first, then we can add fuzzy matching later
    JoinedWithAssignments = Table.NestedJoin(ChargeData, {"Officer Name"}, 
                                           AssignmentData, {"PATROL_MEMBER"}, 
                                           "AssignmentInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    
    // Expand assignment information
    ExpandedAssignments = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithAssignments, "AssignmentInfo", 
        {"PATROL_MEMBER", "ASSIGNMENT", "RANK", "BADGE#", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit Group"}, 
        {"Matched_Officer_Name", "Assignment", "Rank", "Badge_Number", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit_Group"}),
    
    // Add data quality indicators
    AddedQuality = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedAssignments, "Match_Status", each 
        if [Matched_Officer_Name] = null then "Unmatched Officer"
        else "Matched", type text),
    
    // Add citation count for analysis
    AddedCount = Table.AddColumn(AddedQuality, "Citation_Count", each 1, Int64.Type)
in
    AddedCount

// ===================================================================
// QUERY 5: MONTHLY_SUMMONS_SUMMARY
// Executive dashboard summary matching your monthly report format
// ===================================================================

let
    InfoCopData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS"]}[Content],
    CurrentMonth = Date.Month(Date.From(DateTime.LocalNow())),
    CurrentYear = Date.Year(Date.From(DateTime.LocalNow())),
    
    // Filter to current month
    CurrentMonthData = Table.SelectRows(InfoCopData, each [Year] = CurrentYear and [Month] = CurrentMonth),
    
    // Summary by summons type
    SummaryByType = Table.Group(CurrentMonthData, {"Summons Type"}, {
        {"Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // Summary by division
    SummaryByDivision = Table.Group(CurrentMonthData, {"Platoon"}, {
        {"Parking_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "P")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Moving_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "M")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Special_Count", each List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(_, each [Summons Type] = "C")[Count] ? ? {0}), Int64.Type},
        {"Total_Count", each Table.RowCount(_), Int64.Type}
    }),
    
    // Create final summary matching report format
    FinalSummary = Table.FromRows({
        {"Parking Summons", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "P")[Count] ? ? {0})},
        {"Non-Parking Summons", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "M")[Count] ? ? {0})},
        {"Special Complaints", List.Sum(Table.SelectRows(SummaryByType, each [Summons Type] = "C")[Count] ? ? {0})}
    }, {"Summons Type", "Count"})
in
    FinalSummary

## Response:

Perfect!

I can see the issue. The error shows:

**"We couldn't find an Excel table named 'INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE'"**

This is because the `INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS` query is trying to reference a table that doesn't exist yet in **this** Power BI file. ## **ğŸ”§ QUICK FIX:**

**Change the reference in the `INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS` query:**

1. **Right-click** `INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS` â†’ **Edit Query**
2. **Advanced Editor**
3. **Find this line:**
   ```powerquery
   ChargeData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content],
   ```

4. **Change it to:**
   ```powerquery
   ChargeData = INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE,
   ```

5. **Find this line:**
   ```powerquery
   AssignmentData = Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT"]}[Content],
   ```

6. **Change it to:**
   ```powerquery
   AssignmentData = SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT,
   ```

## **ğŸ“‹ CORRECTED FULL QUERY:**

**Fixed INFOCOP Integrated Summons Query**

````powerquery
// 2025-06-14-19-36-17 (EST)
// Police_Analytics/Fixed_INFOCOP_Integrated_Summons
// Author: R. A. Carucci
// Purpose: Fixed version that references Power BI queries instead of Excel tables

let
    // Reference the actual Power BI queries (not Excel tables)
    ChargeData = INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE,
    AssignmentData = SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT,
    
    // Simple join with assignment data using officer names
    JoinedWithAssignments = Table.NestedJoin(ChargeData, {"Officer Name"}, 
                                           AssignmentData, {"PATROL_MEMBER"}, 
                                           "AssignmentInfo", JoinKind.LeftOuter),
    
    // Expand assignment information
    ExpandedAssignments = Table.ExpandTableColumn(JoinedWithAssignments, "AssignmentInfo", 
        {"PATROL_MEMBER", "ASSIGNMENT", "RANK", "BADGE#", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit Group"}, 
        {"Matched_Officer_Name", "Assignment", "Rank", "Badge_Number", "Platoon", "Squad", "Unit_Group"}),
    
    // Add data quality indicators
    AddedQuality = Table.AddColumn(ExpandedAssignments, "Match_Status", each 
        if [Matched_Officer_Name] = null then "Unmatched Officer"
        else "Matched", type text),
    
    // Add citation count for analysis
    AddedCount = Table.AddColumn(AddedQuality, "Citation_Count", each 1, Int64.Type)
in
    AddedCount
````

## **ğŸ’¡ THE ISSUE EXPLAINED:**

The original query used:
```powerquery
Excel.CurrentWorkbook(){[Name="INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE"]}[Content]
```

This looks for an **Excel table** named "INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE" in the current workbook. But in Power BI, we reference other **queries** directly:
```powerquery
INFOCOP_OFFICER_CHARGE_TYPE
```

The `INFOCOP_INTEGRATED_SUMMONS` query should:

### **STEP 1: Create `SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT`**
1. **Get Data** â†’ **Blank Query**
2. **Advanced Editor** â†’ **Delete all code**
3. **Paste this code** from the attached document:

```powerquery
let
    Source = Excel.Workbook(File.Contents("C:\\Users\\carucci_r\\OneDrive - City of Hackensack\\_Hackensack_Data_Repository\\2025_Department_Full_List.xlsx"), null, true),
    
    // Load the PLATOONS table
    PlatoonsData = Source{[Item="PLATOONS",Kind="Table"]}[Data],
    
    // Clean data types
    CleanedTypes = Table.TransformColumnTypes(PlatoonsData,{
        {"PATROL_MEMBER", type text},
        {"ASSIGNMENT", type text},
        {"ASSIGNMENT2", type text},
        {"RANK", type text},
        {"BADGE#", type text},
        {"BADGE2", type text}
    }),
    
    // Normalize badge numbers to 4-digit format for joining
    NormalizedBadges = Table.TransformColumns(CleanedTypes, {
        {"BADGE#", each Text.PadStart(Text.Clean(Text.Trim(Text.From(_))), 4, "0"), type text}
    }),
    
    // Add platoon groupings based on assignment
    WithPlatoon = Table.AddColumn(NormalizedBadges, "Platoon", each 
        if Text.StartsWith([ASSIGNMENT], "A") then "Platoon A"
        else if Text.StartsWith([ASSIGNMENT], "B") then "Platoon B" 
        else if Text.StartsWith([ASSIGNMENT], "C") then "Platoon C"
        else if [ASSIGNMENT] = "TRF" then "Traffic"
        else if Text.StartsWith([ASSIGNMENT], "TCA") then "Traffic"
        else if [ASSIGNMENT] = "STA" then "School Threat Assessment"
        else if [ASSIGNMENT] = "CSB" then "Crime Suppression Bureau" 
        else if [ASSIGNMENT] = "DET" then "Detectives"
        else if [ASSIGNMENT] = "HACSOC" then "Special Operations"
        else if Text.Contains([RANK] ? ? "", "LT") then "Supervision"
        else if Text.Contains([RANK] ? ? "", "CAPT") then "Command"
        else "Other", type text),
    
    WithSquad = Table.AddColumn(WithPlatoon, "Squad", each [ASSIGNMENT], type text),
    
    WithUnitGroup = Table.AddColumn(WithSquad, "Unit Group", each 
        if [Platoon] = "Traffic" then "Enforcement"
        else if Text.Contains([Platoon], "Platoon") then "Patrol"
        else if [Platoon] = "Detectives" then "Investigations" 
        else if [Platoon] = "Supervision" then "Management"
        else if [Platoon] = "Command" then "Command Staff"
        else "Support", type text)
in
    WithUnitGroup
```

4. **Click Done**
5. **Rename** the query to: `SUMMONS_ASSIGNED_SHIFT`
